                 <div class="elementor-widget-wrap">
                  <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-6e0d270 elementor-widget elementor-widget-global elementor-global-1512 elementor-widget-divider" data-element_type="divider.default" data-id="6e0d270">
                   <div class="elementor-widget-container">
                    <div class="elementor-divider">
                     <span class="elementor-divider-separator">
                     </span>
                    </div>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-0b2c55e elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-element_type="heading.default" data-id="0b2c55e">
                   <div class="elementor-widget-container">
                    <h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">
                     WELCOME TO SEDARU.
                    </h2>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-599535a elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-element_type="text-editor.default" data-id="599535a">
                   <div class="elementor-widget-container">
                    <div class="elementor-text-editor elementor-clearfix">
                     <p>
                      Welcome to Our Company.
                     </p>
                     <p>
                      Since our beginnings as IDModeling in 2004, we’ve been on a mission to own the hydraulic and network modeling space for wet infrastructure, driving utility planning and operations, managing and maximizing enterprise data.
                     </p>
                     <p>
                      This focus inspired a unique perspective on the challenges utilities face to readily access meaningful data to implement critical decisions. This perspective led us to disrupt our business, and the industry, with the development of our software, Sedaru (See Data Run).
                     </p>
                     <p>
                      Sedaru defines the modern utility management system, delivering the singular, exclusive location for our utility customers to access the information, automation, and control of the business and assets they operate.
                     </p>
                     <p>
                      We look forward to understanding your unique challenges, and working together to help advance your utility forward.
                     </p>
                     <p>
                      Thank you for visiting Sedaru.
                     </p>
                    </div>
                   </div>
                  </div>

              <div class="elementor-row">

   <script>
    (function() {function addEventListener(element,event,handler) {
 	if(element.addEventListener) {
 		element.addEventListener(event,handler, false);
 	} else if(element.attachEvent){
 		element.attachEvent('on'+event,handler);
 	}
 }function maybePrefixUrlField() {
 	if(this.value.trim() !== '' && this.value.indexOf('http') !== 0) {
 		this.value = "http://" + this.value;
 	}
 }
 
 var urlFields = document.querySelectorAll('.mc4wp-form input[type="url"]');
 if( urlFields && urlFields.length > 0 ) {
 	for( var j=0; j < urlFields.length; j++ ) {
 		addEventListener(urlFields[j],'blur',maybePrefixUrlField);
 	}
 }/* test if browser supports date fields */
 var testInput = document.createElement('input');
 testInput.setAttribute('type', 'date');
 if( testInput.type !== 'date') {
 
 	/* add placeholder & pattern to all date fields */
 	var dateFields = document.querySelectorAll('.mc4wp-form input[type="date"]');
 	for(var i=0; i<dateFields.length; i++) {
 		if(!dateFields[i].placeholder) {
 			dateFields[i].placeholder = 'YYYY-MM-DD';
 		}
 		if(!dateFields[i].pattern) {
 			dateFields[i].pattern = '[0-9]{4}-(0[1-9]|1[012])-(0[1-9]|1[0-9]|2[0-9]|3[01])';
 		}
 	}
 }
 
 })();
   </script>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    function revslider_showDoubleJqueryError(sliderID) {
 					var errorMessage = "Revolution Slider Error: You have some jquery.js library include that comes after the revolution files js include.";
 					errorMessage += "<br> This includes make eliminates the revolution slider libraries, and make it not work.";
 					errorMessage += "<br><br> To fix it you can:<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 1. In the Slider Settings -> Troubleshooting set option:  <strong><b>Put JS Includes To Body</b></strong> option to true.";
 					errorMessage += "<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 2. Find the double jquery.js include and remove it.";
 					errorMessage = "<span style='font-size:16px;color:#BC0C06;'>" + errorMessage + "</span>";
 						jQuery(sliderID).show().html(errorMessage);
 				}
   </script>
